THE COMMISSIONER OF LAND ADMINISTRATION CHEPAUK, CHENNAI-600 005.
ACQUISITION OF LANDS
FORM - C
[See Rule 7]
NOTICE UNDER SUB-SECTION (1) OF SECTION 3 OF THE TAMIL NADU ACQUISITION OF LAND FOR 
INDUSTRIAL PURPOSES ACT, 1997
(CLA-TID/2025/03/01/01/0001)
No.VI(1)/130(b-1)/2025.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be 
acquired for industrial purpose to wit to TIDCO - New Green Field Airport and it having already been decided that 
the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by 
the Managing Director, TIDCO. The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu 
Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule 
below measuring an extent of 12.3450 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
TIDCO - New Green Field Airport.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Kancheepuram and Special Tahsildar(LA), 
Unit, Kancheepuram which may be inspected on any day during office hours.

TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY	
5
(CLA-TID/2025/03/06/27/0001)
No.VI(1)/130(b-2)/2025.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be acquired 
for industrial purpose to wit to TIDCO - New Green Field Airport and it having already been decided that the amount 
of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the Managing 
Director, TIDCO. The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land 
for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 13.1950 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
TIDCO - New Green Field Airport.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Kancheepuram and Special Tahsildar(LA), 
Unit, Kancheepuram which may be inspected on any day during office hours.
The Schedule
Kancheepuram District, Sriperumbudur Taluk, Magadevimangalam Village.

No.VI(1)/130(b-3)/2025.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be 
acquired for industrial purpose to wit to TIDCO - New Green Field Airport and it having already been decided that 
the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by 
the Managing Director, TIDCO. The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu 
Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999).
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule 
below measuring an extent of 10.3850 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
TIDCO - New Green Field Airport. 
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO (LA), Kancheepuram and Special Tahsildar (LA), 
Unit, Kancheepuram which may be inspected on any day during office hours.

Total extent to be acquired : 10.3850 (Hectares)
(CLA-TID/2025/03/08/40/0001)
No.VI(1)/130(b-4)/2025.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be 
acquired for industrial purpose to wit to TIDCO - New Green Field Airport and it having already been decided that 
the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by 
the Managing Director, TIDCO. The following notice is issued under sub-section (1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu 
Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule 
below measuring an extent of 6.1467 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
TIDCO - New Green Field Airport.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO (LA), Kancheepuram and Special Tahsildar (LA), 
Unit, Kancheepuram which may be inspected on any day during office hours.

No.VI(1)/130(b-5)/2025.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be acquired 
for industrial purpose to wit to TIDCO - New Green Field Airport and it having already been decided that the amount 
of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the Managing 
Director, TIDCO. The following notice is issued under sub-section (1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of 
Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule 
below measuring an extent of 14.0450 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, 
for TIDCO - New Green Field Airport.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO (LA), Kancheepuram and Special Tahsildar (LA), 
Unit, Kancheepuram which may be inspected on any day during office hours.

TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY	
43
(LA-I(1)/9557576/2025)
No.VI(1)/130(b-8)/2025.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below to be 
acquired for Industrial Purposes to wit for the Doubling of Broad-Gauge Railway Line between Eraniel and Parassala 
in Nalloor Village of Vilavancode Taluk in Kanniyakumari District, and it having already been decided that the amount 
of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by Southern 
Railways. The following notice is issued under sub-section (1) of Section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for 
Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule 
below measuring 65324 Sq.mtrs., to the same, a little more or less needed for Industrial Purpose to wit for the Doubling 
of Broad-Gauge Railway Line between Eraniel and Parassala in Nalloor Village of Vilavancode Taluk in Kanniyakumari 
District.
The plan of the lands are kept in the Office of the District Collector, Kanniyakumari District which may be inspected 
at any time during office hours.
The Schedule
Kanniyakumari District, Vilavancode Taluk, Nalloor Village.

(LA-I(1)/9602042/2025)
No.VI(1)/130(b-9)/2025.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below to be acquired 
for Industrial Purposes to wit to Doubling of Broad-Gauge Railway Line from Omalur to Mettur Dam in P.N. Patti and 
M. Kalipatti Villages of Mettur Taluk in Salem District, and it having already been decided that the amount of compensation 
to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by Southern Railways. The following 
notice is issued under sub-section (1) of Section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 
1997 (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring 624 Sq.mtrs., to the same, a little more or less needed for Industrial Purpose wit, for the Doubling of Broad-
Gauge Railway Line from Omalur to Mettur Dam in  P.N. Patti and M. Kalipatti Villages of Mettur Taluk in Salem District.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Land Acquisition Officer / District Revenue Officer, Salem which 
may be inspected on any day during office hours.

 The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below to be acquired 
for Highways Department to wit for the formation of Varanasi – Kanyakumari Road (Abandoned NH-SHU 73) for the 
Construction of Flyover in Goripalayam Junction East Madurai Village in the Taluk of Madurai South and the Villages 
of North Madurai, Bibikulam in the Taluk of Madurai North, Madurai District and it having already been decided that the 
entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by 
Highways Department. The following notice is issued under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways 
Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu is hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below measuring an extent of 5235.8 Sq.mtrs., 
to the same, a little more or less needed for  Highways purpose, to wit for the formation of Varanasi – Kanyakumari 
Road (Abandoned NH-SHU 73) for the Construction of Flyover in Goripalayam Junction in East Madurai Village in the 
Taluk of Madurai South and the Villages of North Madurai, Bibikulam in the Taluk of Madurai North, Madurai District.
The plan of the lands is kept in the office of the Special District Revenue Officer, (LA), Highways and office of 
the Special Tahsildar (LA), Highways Unit -1, Collectorate campus, New Building, Madurai – 20 may be inspected on 
any day during office hours.

Total extent of lands to be acquired 5235.8 Square meters
(LA- VI(3)/9026556/2024)  
No.VI(1)/130(b-11)/2025.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below to be acquired 
for Highways Department to wit for the Construction of Grade Seperator including Junction Improvement of Madurai 
- Thondi Road (SH-33) Madurai Town  of Madurai North Taluk, Madurai  District and it having already been decided 
that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or 
managed by Highways Department. The following notice is issued under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil 
Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the 
Governor of Tamil Nadu is hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below measuring an extent of 2050 
Sq.mtrs., to the same, a little more or less needed for  Highways purpose, to wit for the Construction of Grade Separator 
including Junction Improvement of Madurai - Thondi Road (SH-33) in Madurai Town (Sathamangalam, Managiri Bit-1) 
Madurai North Taluk, Madurai  District.
The plan of the lands is kept in the office of the Special District Revenue Officer, (LA), Highways and office of the 
Special Tahsildar (LA), Highways Unit -2, Collector campus, New Building, Madurai – 20 may be inspected on any 
day during office hours.

No.VI(1)/130(b-12)/2025.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Scheduled below have to be 
acquired the Wet & Dry lands for the formation of Bypass Road between Manalurpettai Road-Kallakurichi Road in 
Melkachirapattu-Kilkachirapattu Bypass in the Melkachirapattu Village,  Tiruvannamalai Taluk & District and it having 
already been decided that the entire amount of compensations to be awarded for the land is to be paid out of the 
funds controlled and managed by the Highways Department. The following notice under sub-section 1 of Section 15 
of Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34/2002).
NOTICE
	
Under sub-section 1 of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34/2002) the 
Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the Lands specified in the schedule below measuring an extent of 10935 
Square Meters of Wet & Dry lands for the formation of Bypass Road between Manalurpettai Road-Kallakurichi Road 
in Melkachirapattu-Kilkachirapattu Bypass in Melkachirapattu Village, Tiruvannamalai Taluk & District, to the same a 
little more or less needed for Highways Purposes.

(CLA-SIP/2025/28/01/08/0001)
No.VI(1)/130(b-14)/2025.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be acquired 
for industrial purpose to wit to SIPCOT - Establishment of Solar Power Plant and it having already been decided 
that the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed 
by the Managing Director, SIPCOT. The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu 
Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Lands for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 4.7950 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for SIPCOT - 
Establishment of Solar Power Plant.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tirunelveli and Special Tahsildar(LA), Unit 
,Tirunelveli which may be inspected on any day during office hours.

(CLA-SIP/2025/40/06/05/0001)
No.VI(1)/130(b-16)/2025.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be acquired 
for industrial purpose to wit to SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park and it having already been decided that the amount 
of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the Managing 
Director, SIPCOT. The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of 
Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Lands for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997(Tamil Nadu 
Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below measuring an 
extent of 10.8600 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for SIPCOT - SIPCOT 
Industrial Park.
  The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvallur and Special Tahsildar(LA), Unit , 
Tiruvallur which may be inspected on any day during office hours.
